padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2318698">posiechemist_</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-14">11/14/24 00:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm going to be the black sheep here but hear me out...<br />
As a woman, I absolutely love this perfume! It's my boyfriend's, but all I am doing lately is to try out his perfumes to test their longevity, sillage and how they perform on my skin. Let's just say...I'm in my self-discovery era, where I don't let "male" or "female" label what I like.<br />
<br />
All I can say...is that I have no idea what people on here are on about this being a summer perfume. Don't get me wrong, I understand that the majority of these notes will perform better in humid and warm conditions. BUT, for me, this perfume sits in the extremes : either in a hot summer evening, or in a cold humid winter day, this perfume is easily one of my favorite because how it makes ME feel. <br />
<br />
I get why this is labeled as "summer". The coconutty, pineapple-y notes surely do make your mind think about a fruity cocktail on the beach, but the woodsy, tonka notes that I personally detect on my skin after it's sat for a few hours, give me a cozy, warm, fuzzy-sweater vibes. <br />
<br />
Conclusion: don't let labels keep you from smelling lovely perfumes and just wear whatever the heck you want, whener you want.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2348398"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2348398#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2348032" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
TLDR: its a somewhat mass appealing woody take on le beau edt that has an amazing smell, better projection and longevity and overall value. recommend buying IF the smell is not repulsing as it is for a few people. 4.5/5<br />
<br />
you can already see the notes on the website. but if i had to describe it in my own words:<br />
<br />
- welcoming<br />
- warm<br />
- rich sweetness<br />
- tropical, but not ocean. more like the beach with the palm trees and flowers before the water.<br />
- a lighter type of wood<br />
- calm type of flower<br />
<br />
scent: 4.5/5 (try it for yourself, not a 5 because it's not extremely mass appealing, but for the most part people can appreciate this scent)<br />
projection: 4/5 (think wingspan range)<br />
longevity: 4/5 (it can project well for minimum 8 hours thanks to a stronger formulation)<br />
price: 3/5 (of course people will want it to be cheaper. but when you realize the uniqueness of this fragrance and what it does, you can see how the pricing is appropriate. worth it, but not like a bargain. you get what you pay for type of transaction)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2306704" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="tcd54"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2170836"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2170836.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="tcd54" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2306704ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2306704" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87); tropical scent. Coconutty, woody and vanillic. It’s quite creamy and dense so It should work well year round but i’d probably avoid in really high heat. Is it synthetic smelling? Yes, very much so, but I couldn’t care less. I’m not one of these snobs that completely writes off scents because they aren’t packed to the brim with naturals. I love this stuff, It’s very addictive and when caught by the wind gives you these gorgeous whiffs. It’s a pretty unique fragrance among other designers that i’ve tried so you’ll most likely be pulling a good bit of attention with this. Performance is as good as you’d ever want it to be with this type of scent. Will easily last all day and project well for quite a while. I love how the liquid is blue. When I go to spritz my tester bottle on the colour of the juice just makes it feel that much more refreshing. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2221719">Fragance_Snow</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-04">09/04/24 14:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Honest Review (8.5/10):<br />
<br />
JPG- Le Beau Le Parfum🍍🪻🥥 has a rich strong opening (unlike the critic component in the EDT or the minty aquatic of Paradise Garden) that has pineapple, iris &amp; woody notes. I can’t identify the ginger in the smell but it’s cited as one of the opening notes. Le Parfum is the longer lasting among the 3. The smell transitions into a rich ambery’ one containing sandalwood.<br />
<br />
I get ppl that don’t find occasion for this fragrance. I can use it almost all year bc i live in a tropical country. Could be overpowering in the hottest days of summer if over-sprayed. Generally speaking It’s better for spring, summer nights and fall.<br />
<br />
I find it the most mature fragrance in the Le Beau line. Again generally speaking, I think most fragrances within the JPG brand are sweet (like Le Male Elixir, all le beau and even scandal Absolu) so try it on your skin before buying. <br />
<br />
Regards,<br />
Snow</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2271654"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2271654#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2268882" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I want to. But I don’t. <br />
<br />
I blind bought this after all the hype, how can so many people be wrong, I thought. I wanted something for summer, for everyday, fresh and seductive, a jack of all trades… this was going to be that. Honestly, I find it mediocre, unremarkable, and, at times, bad, like sweaty smelling bad. <br />
<br />
The bottle is pleasant, I usually find JPG bottles too loud and cheap looking (shoot me, but I do, grow up!)… but this bottle looks classy enough on the shelf. Therein ends my interest in this. Maybe it’s for a younger crowd (I’m nearly 40). Maybe it’s just not for me. But amongst my Tom Ford, Chanel, Valentino, Dior, etc, this stands no chance. It’s a boy amongst men. <br />
<br />
Overall, I’d rate this 6/10… and I’m being nice, because I’m a nice guy! Would pass, will likely sell, and I’ve never in my life sold a perfume!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2258716"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2258716#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2258664" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; But in some way it raises no emotions in me. Feels like a simulation of a deep, non-aquatic summer scent; like someone prompted an AI with "create a perfume in the style of le male le parfum, but for summer".<br />
<br />
My main issue is the lack of occasions to actually wear this. Its natural habitat seems to be summer nights having drinks outside with a multicolored shirt on. And even then I'd choose a fragrance with a little more spice and freshness. For a hot summer day it feels too sweet and somewhat powdery. Este todoterreno del mundo de los perfumes es conocido por su tropical y distintivo aroma de salida a "piña colada". Con una madera masculina y dulce presente en todo momento, cambia rápidamente a un coco sexy y dulce que se huele a metros de distancia, llenando la habitación. Un consejo que he tenido que descubrir por las malas, no use el dicho perfume las dos semanas después de haber bebido demasiado alcohol, pues éste altera temporalmente la percepción de las fragancias, y puede desembocar en que usted perciba el perfume como con un hedor a vómito que no podrá quitarse de la cabeza.<br />

Diseño de botella: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐<br />
Aroma: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐<br />
Climas: 🍁 - ❄️ - 🌸 - ⛱️<br />

Summer wear?  Questionable, but yes you can pull it off all year.<br />

<br />
Mind you, I base my compliment guage off Rasasi Hawas (THE MOST COMPLIMENTED IN MY 20 FRAG COLLECTION). In comparison to Hawas, this gets very little compliments.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2217524"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2217524#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2216924" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; There is a reason you can’t find this anywhere</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2216924"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2216924#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2214744" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2214744" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="bunn100"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2129907"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2129907.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="bunn100" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2214744ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2214744" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2129907">bunn100</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-10">07/10/24 20:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This scent is designed to make you feel like a Greek god—specifically one that enjoys a cheeky wink and a flirty smile. But does it really deliver, or is it just another pretty bottle on the shelf?<br />
<br />
The bottle is a sculpted masterpiece—a torso of a man that looks like it’s been chiseled by the gods themselves. It’s bold, shiny, and demands attention, like a peacock at a pigeon party. But don’t be fooled by its stunning exterior; we need to know if the juice inside matches the glamour on the outside.<br />
<br />
Scent Profile<br />
Le Beau Le Parfum opens with a burst of coconut, pineapple, and tonka bean. Imagine you’re at a tropical beach party where someone’s passing around a piña colada and yelling, “Surf’s up!” It’s sweet, fruity, and makes you want to put on sunglasses even if you’re indoors.<br />
<br />
As the top notes mellow, you’re greeted by a blend of jasmine, iris, and geranium. It’s like a bouquet of flowers just showed up at the beach, slightly confusing the vibe but adding a touch of elegance. It’s floral but not overpowering, like someone brought a classy date to a luau.<br />
<br />
The dry down features sandalwood, ambergris, and vanilla. Now you’re chilling by a bonfire, the scent of warm woods and sweet vanilla swirling around you. It’s cozy, inviting, and makes you want to wrap yourself in a blanket and tell stories under the stars.<br />
<br />
Longevity and Sillage<br />
Le Beau Le Parfum has the staying power of a dedicated partygoer—it lasts a good 6-8 hours. It’s not the longest-lasting fragrance out there, but it won’t leave you hanging after an hour either. The sillage is moderate to strong; you’ll leave a noticeable trail, but it’s more of a gentle wave than a tidal surge. People will definitely notice you, but you won’t be overwhelming anyone’s nostrils.<br />
<br />
This fragrance is versatile enough for various occasions, it’s perfect for date nights, parties, or anytime you want to feel like the best-looking guy in the room. Just don’t wear it to the gym unless you want to be “that guy.”<br />
<br />
Overall Impressions<br />
Le Beau Le Parfum is for the man who wants to smell as good as he looks. It’s charming, flirty, and just a bit cheeky—perfect for turning heads without being too in-your-face.<br />
<br />
In conclusion, Le Beau Le Parfum by Jean Paul Gaultier is like a well-dressed charmer at a beach party—fun, attractive, and likely to make a lasting impression. It’s perfect for those who want a bit of tropical flair with a touch of class. So spritz it on, strut your stuff, and enjoy the attention. Just remember, not everyone will be dazzled by your coconut-infused confidence—but hey, you can’t win them all!<br />
<br />
Sniff-O-Meter Score<br />
<br />
Scent Appeal: 4 - “Sexy and captivating, like a flirtatious wink.”<br />
Longevity: 3 - “Holds on well, but not an all-day powerhouse.”<br />
Sillage: 4 - “Creates a noticeable, yet not overwhelming presence.”<br />
Uniqueness: 4 - “Distinctive and alluring, with a strong character.”<br />
Versatility: 3 - “Good for most occasions, but can be a bit intense for every day.”<br />
<br />
Overall Sniff-O-Meter Score: 18/25</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2214744"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2214744#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2214502" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2202054" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RawBeans1"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2179089"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="RawBeans1" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2202054ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2202054" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2179089">RawBeans1</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-28">06/28/24 09:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The longevity of the fragrance is excellent. Note that the scent changes slightly depending on whether you apply it to your clothing or your skin. This is due to your skin's pH and possibly other factors, but fortunately, both smelled great to me. The scent on my skin lasts over 8 hours, while the scent on the clothes I sprayed yesterday is still noticeable, so it easily lasts more than a day (I only sprayed once on each side of my clothes to test its duration). Compared to Le Beau EDT, this fragrance is more intense and has a darker scent. I slightly prefer the initial spray of the EDT over the Le Parfum, but that's just for the first 3-5 minutes. Overall, I enjoy both fragrances, but in my opinion, Le Beau Le Parfum is better. I'm not a fragrance expert, but if you're considering buying this and you like a sweet fragrance with a bit of darkness from the woody notes, I would suggest buying it. If you're more apprehensive, get a sample and test it on yourself before purchasing.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2202054"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2202054#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2201906" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2201906"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2201906#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2201836" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2201836" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="sidalwayssmellsgood"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2001234"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2001234.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="sidalwayssmellsgood" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2201836ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2201836" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2001234">sidalwayssmellsgood</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-28">06/28/24 04:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I see a lot of praises for this one here. Let me voice my opinion: the EDT is better by a mile. It’s not bad. But it’s not the EDT.<br />
<br />
There are several issues I have with this:<br />
(1) The purpose of a tropical summery fragrance is to be light and breezy without being cloying or harsh. The daytime heat makes a fragrance radiate far stronger than post-sundown. To make a formulation stronger by dialling every element of the fragrance up without any consideration for this might just make a fragrance like this go nuts.<br />
(2) What is that lemongrass/green tea/ginger note that’s so synthetic and making the fragrance smell like it wants to claw my face off?<br />
(3) Take the aforementioned disturbing note away, and it is basically the EDT in a lesser, more appropriate concentration, which doesn’t perform much worse than Le Parfum.<br />
<br />
Moral of the story: higher concentration doesn’t always mean better. Save your money, get the EDT while you can.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2201836"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2201836#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2201362" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

Scent: 9/10<br />
Projection: 9.5/10<br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2180335" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Armani34"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2031860"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2031860.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Armani34" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2180335ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2180335" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2031860">Armani34</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-06">06/06/24 14:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Le Beau Le Parfum!!<br />
Una joya de perfume,se abre con una piña especiada,con cipres y un iris totalmente diferente al iris de Dior o Prada,este iris es terroso,para nada se huele a maquillaje o lapiz labial,para nada,Jean Paul Gaultier trabaja el iris de forma diferente,lo hacen terroso,<br />
En su corazon sale el coco amaderado,q al mezclarse con la piña especiada por el jengibre da una vibra de piña colada,densa algo terrosa,una delicia,<br />
En el.corazon el famoso Haba Tonka y el Ambar toman el control del secado,siendo este uno dulzon,tambien se siente una cremosidad q es por el Sandalo q da esa imprecion de cremosidad,tambien se siente el Ambar Gris,su secado es una combinacion de haba tonka,ambar y ambar gris,estos 3 juntos aportan esa dulzura,pero q en mi opinion no es empalagosa para nada,y cremoso por el sandalo,creo q se mantiene fuera de lo empalagoso y para mi creo q se debe al iris terroso y al cipres,creo q estos 2 ingredientes le dan el balance para q no sea empalagoso,eso si yo lo uso en el verano en las noches,no me veo con esto puesto de dia a 98 grados Farenheith,ahora esto es un perfume nocturno,fiestero q te traera cumplido!!<br />
La duracion es buenisima en mi caso,despues de una noche de jangueo en el vlub,de bailar y sudar,al terminar la noche y regresar a mi casa todavia siento el perfume en una burbuja personal q todavia esta lejos de estar al raz de piel,diria q la burbuja q me deja ya cuando llego a mi casa es de un pies pies y medio,q conste q eso es luego de janguear toda la noche de bailar,sudar,parame frente a los abanicos gigantes para refrescarme,osea q en cuestion despues de practicamente desmadrar el perfume y como quiera me da ese rendimiento,<br />
La proyeccion en una muuuyyy buena,no diria q modo bestia,pero es muy buena en mi caso,de la estela q va dejando no tengo mucha infor.acion para compartir con ustedes lo q si me ha pasado es q se me han acercado personas a las q le pase por el lado a decirme q he dejado un olor divino cuando pase por sus lados,pero no me fije cuan cerca o lejos se encontraban esas personas pq han sido varios,y la gente se anima a acercarse a mi y hablarme del perfume q traigo puesto pues muchisima gente donde soy saben q soy amante a los perfumes,gente q me conoce bien y gente q no me conoce tan bien!!!<br />
<br />
Le Beau Le Parfum 9.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2180335"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2180335#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2180141" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2174746" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Aromaventure"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2152922"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2152922.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Aromaventure" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2174746ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2174746" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2152922">Aromaventure</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-01">06/01/24 12:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Review of Le Beau Le Parfum by Jean Paul Gaultier<br />
<br />
Introduction<br />
<br />
Le Beau Le Parfum by Jean Paul Gaultier is a captivating addition to the iconic designer's fragrance collection. This eau de parfum is a richer, more intense interpretation of the original Le Beau, offering a blend of aromatic and woody notes that are both alluring and sophisticated. Launched in 2022, it continues to embody the brand's daring and seductive ethos.<br />
<br />
Packaging and Presentation<br />
<br />
The presentation of Le Beau Le Parfum is a feast for the eyes. The bottle, shaped like a sculpted male torso, is a testament to Jean Paul Gaultier's signature style. Adorned with a fig leaf, it symbolizes both sensuality and elegance, making it a striking addition to any fragrance collection. The deep green hue of the glass suggests the richness and depth of the scent within.<br />
<br />
Scent Profile<br />
<br />
Top Notes: The fragrance opens with a vibrant burst of fresh, citrusy bergamot paired with the sweet and slightly spicy allure of ginger. This invigorating combination immediately captures the senses, creating an inviting and energetic start.<br />
<br />
Heart Notes: As the top notes mellow, the heart reveals a harmonious blend of coconut wood and Tonka bean. The coconut wood adds a creamy, exotic touch, while the Tonka bean brings a warm, vanilla-like sweetness. This interplay creates a smooth and seductive middle phase that is both comforting and intriguing.<br />
<br />
Base Notes: The dry-down is where Le Beau Le Parfum truly shines. The base is composed of ambergris and sandalwood, providing a rich, earthy foundation. Ambergris imparts a subtle marine nuance, adding depth and complexity, while sandalwood delivers a creamy, woody finish that lingers beautifully on the skin.<br />
<br />
Longevity and Sillage<br />
<br />
Le Beau Le Parfum boasts impressive longevity, easily lasting throughout the day with just a few sprays. Its sillage is moderate to strong, ensuring that the wearer leaves a memorable trail without overwhelming those nearby. This balance makes it suitable for both daytime and evening wear, offering versatility for various occasions.<br />
<br />
Versatility and Occasions<br />
<br />
This fragrance is versatile enough to be worn in a variety of settings. Its fresh and inviting top notes make it appropriate for daytime use, while the deeper, more sensual base notes render it perfect for evening events and intimate gatherings. Le Beau Le Parfum is particularly well-suited for cooler weather, where its warm and spicy elements can truly shine.<br />
<br />
Conclusion<br />
<br />
Le Beau Le Parfum by Jean Paul Gaultier is a masterfully crafted fragrance that exudes confidence and charm. Its well-balanced composition of fresh, woody, and sweet notes ensures it appeals to a wide audience, while its striking bottle design adds a touch of luxury. Whether you're a long-time fan of the brand or new to Jean Paul Gaultier's fragrances, Le Beau Le Parfum is a worthy addition to any collection, offering a bold yet refined olfactory experience.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Very unique and quite different from the other fragrances of this line. I wear this all year through, even in Wintertime if I'm out to have some fun. Longevity is good, both on my skin and on my clothes. Sillage is quite good as well. It is one of the fragrances that people regularly ask me what I am wearing, both men and women. I imagine that I'll be buying this one for forever, because of how I love this fragrance and its uniqueness. Though, I will only buy it when I spot it at a discounter: he price is on the high side, but that's JPG for you. The new Paradise Garden is very much in line with this one, and I might switch between it now and then.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2170341"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2170341#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2168817" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
This is a nice beach vibe scent. But it's an EDT in performance. Skin close almost immediately. The list of scents I'd give a shot before settling for this is long. Lattafa's Asad (pretty much an Aventus clone), Armaf's Club de Nuit Intense Man Parfum, Mancera's Coco Vanille, Margiela's Beach Walk, Nishane's Hacivat and Fan Your Flames, Kilian's Moonlight in Heaven. All have this sort of vibe, all but Beach Walk perform better. The only JPG scent I have yet to try is the Scandal Pour Homme Le Parfum. I have a sample when I get around to it. But I expect the same disappointing potency as the other Jean Paul Gaultier scents, and it's a damn shame because I really like the scents. They're all nice, but they don't project and they don't endure, and every time they release a new scent I hope for better performance, but never get it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Smell: A tropical, unformal type smell. It has the woods, the coconut, pineapple, some fruits, a bit synthetic but very, very nice. Piña colada at the beach vibe. Some people wear it in winter due to strength and the fact that it's a heavy fragrance, but just such a nice tropical vibe.<br />
Performance: Extreme. 4 sprays, at the most. Any more and the smell will be overpowering, due to its strength. Even two sprays will be enough to get smelled. Also the lasting, which is very good. Lasts around 7-8 hours and my friend was still complimenting me.<br />

Le Male Elixir. This fragrance being sweet with a woodsy accord follows me into that category.<br />
<br />
Sprayed this on to wear for my first time owning it yesterday &amp; was given the compliment of it being related to those two fragrances &amp; honestly I can smell those in this one. Getting whiffs of it on my neck got me the smell of 1M Lucky &amp; its laying sweet tone of Le Male Elixir. Kind of if they had a baby. Overall, pleasant fragrance but not overwhelming as much. Definitely need a sweet tooth for this one. Suited for spring &amp; fall, summer evenings. It is a common misconception that this is a summer fragrance &amp; it is NOT. I can see this fragrance being cloying in high heat.<br />
<br />
Definitely lean for something more fresh if you are looking to buy this as a "summer" scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="2153600"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=2153600#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2152914" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1266523">Seuni</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-02-12">02/12/22 13:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>So, I actually own it, a 125ml bought locally at Douglas. Not a troll here.<br />
<br />
The opening is strong. The iris is not super strong - it's most about the pineapple and coconut sandalwood based combo, but the iris smells like the one in Le Male le Parfum. Looks like the le Parfum flankers are goinng to be stronger with the addition of iris. Like Allure Edition Blanche this is complimented by sandalwood in the base, introducing creamy, sweet, gourmand, soapy vibe. The sandalwood, coconut, and pineapple mix gives a very apparent and strong Piña Colada smell.<br />
<br />
The way the sandalwood mixes with iris, woodsy notes and summer character makes it a sweet, creamy, woody, soapy vibe. I kid you not - this smells like Dove made a Piña Colada fragranced soap.<br />
<br />
I can't say for the performance - i just bought it. I will update this review with the performance as soon as I test it sufficiently (can I have an upvote please ;) ?)<br />
Right now it seems like a strong projection for two hours and moderate later with about 7 hours performance (then becoming a skin scent) and a nice sillage for 3-4.<br />
<br />
This is a sweet summer fragrance loaded with cream, soap, coconut, pineapple - a creamy piña colada. A Dove piña colada fragranced soap. Not office safe I think - a bit too playful <br />
Summer, beach, fun time I think is the best.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="1503117"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=1503117#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1569342" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
It's really different if you compare it to the original and I was surprised (in a good way) about the direction they took it. It's way deeper and heavier than the original with a focus on something woody, sweet with the sandalwood and vanilla and that coconut. There are more nuances to its sweet side than in the original and thus, the coconut comes across as a bit different as well.<br />
<br />
I like it a lot. And it has grown on me even more since my review of it. And it seems like people around me love it even more since I had quite a few compliments when wearing it.<br />
<br />
I usually finish a full bottle of Le Beau every single summer and I have a feeling my 75ml will be at least half full by the end of this summer. And.. Due to it's more deep kind of blend I will definitely use it a lot throughout the year.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="1569342"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=1569342#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1773130" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Pineapple, coconut and tonka bean. It is so smooth and creamy it actually lifts my mood when I wear it.<br />
<br />
Pure luxury. But this is no blind buy; the coconut is very strong but I like it.<br />

Can't think of a single negative for me.<br />
<br />
10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="1773130"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=1773130#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1502900" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1502900" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="masako_30"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1137173"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1137173.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="masako_30" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chloe/Nomade-Nuit-d-Egypte-89372.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.89372.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Nomade Nuit d’Egypte"title="Nomade Nuit d’Egypte"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1502900ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1502900" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1137173">masako_30</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-02-12">02/12/22 06:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>What I didn't expect was its very fruity opening.<br />
Generally I know perfumes in which pineapple is associated with metallic notes, so that it almost disappears. Here the cypress sustains this note but neither obscures nor mineralizes it, therefore is very perceptible.<br />
This version of Le Beau Le Parfum (Edp Intense) is much more masculine than Le Beau, despite the presence of iris and tonka that I feel both faintly.<br />
Coconut also struggles to emerge but helps to soften the base of the perfume, which takes on subtly amber shades. Predominantly, on my female skin the cypress is the main note for a good portion of time, until the drydown that fades into a wonderful soft cloud, slightly almondy, that I can't stop smelling.<br />
Strangely, clothes imprison instead a fruity note similar to mango.<br />
My good impression is that an excellent job and research are behind it so that overall the fragrance took on more decisive shades and a much more refined taste. For also an even more contrast between top notes and drydown, compared to the previous version.<br />
As if usual simple and commonly used notes were in new blend for a more modern symphony.<br />
I have owned it for a day and currently I've got and express a very positive judgment.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72158"comment_id="1502900"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Beau-Le-Parfum-72158.html?ccid=1502900#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2034555" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
